\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01072}01072     \textcolor{comment}{// Determine the decimal exponent. Based on the algorithm by David Gay (https://github.com/jwiegley/gdtoa/blob/master/dtoa.c)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01073}01073     \mbox{\hyperlink{a00105}{double\_cast\_t}} converter = \{ .\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce}{decimal}} = decimalValue \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01074}01074     int32\_t exponentOfTwo = (converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c}{parts}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84}{exponent}} -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a530d18cb538ad15c1217a9eae84f7c3a_a530d18cb538ad15c1217a9eae84f7c3a}{DOUBLE\_EXPONENT\_ZERO\_VALUE}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01075}01075     converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c}{parts}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84}{exponent}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a530d18cb538ad15c1217a9eae84f7c3a_a530d18cb538ad15c1217a9eae84f7c3a}{DOUBLE\_EXPONENT\_ZERO\_VALUE}};  \textcolor{comment}{// drop the exponent so converter.decimal is now in [1,2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01076}01076 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01077}01077     \textcolor{comment}{// now approximate log10 from the log2 integer part and an expansion of ln around 1.5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01078}01078     int32\_t exponentValue = (int32\_t) ((converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce}{decimal}} -\/ 1.5) * \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a4012ed80daeb9d70a23f64f596c7ca53_a4012ed80daeb9d70a23f64f596c7ca53}{LOG\_APPROXIMATION}} + \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a3c180dcf430744c6e184e83134dcf559_a3c180dcf430744c6e184e83134dcf559}{LOG10\_OF\_1\_5}} + exponentOfTwo * \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a717725c873ec28220e835ecc2a97fab5_a717725c873ec28220e835ecc2a97fab5}{LOG10\_OF\_2}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01079}01079     exponentOfTwo = (int32\_t) (exponentValue * \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_aa4aaba3a81c3c56a144bb0d6fe94907b_aa4aaba3a81c3c56a144bb0d6fe94907b}{LOG2\_OF\_10}} + 0.5);  \textcolor{comment}{// now we want to compute 10\string^exponentValue, but we want to be sure it won't overflow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01080}01080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01081}01081     \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} zValue = (exponentValue * \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_ab3ffc1902fe7c3582138db012ba7e63e_ab3ffc1902fe7c3582138db012ba7e63e}{NATURAL\_LOG\_OF\_10}}) -\/ (exponentOfTwo * \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a95d673e706e6582f1a47ab891d75091e_a95d673e706e6582f1a47ab891d75091e}{NATURAL\_LOG\_OF\_2}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01082}01082     \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} zPowOfTwo = zValue * zValue;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01083}01083 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01084}01084     converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c}{parts}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84_a793e594de558979eeb321298231b0a84}{exponent}} += exponentOfTwo;    \textcolor{comment}{// return exp value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01085}01085     converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c_ac1625eb1db6e55ddfc621ab289169c8c}{parts}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a542558132c4e92a5bb73f7470755c3a7_a542558132c4e92a5bb73f7470755c3a7}{mantissa}} = 0;   \textcolor{comment}{// drop mantissa}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01086}01086 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01087}01087     \textcolor{comment}{// compute exp(z) using continued fractions, see https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Exponential\_function\#Continued\_fractions\_for\_ex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01088}01088     converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce}{decimal}} = converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce}{decimal}} * (1 + 2 * zValue / (2 -\/ zValue + (zPowOfTwo / (6 + (zPowOfTwo / (10 + zPowOfTwo / 14))))));}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01089}01089 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01090}01090     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (decimalValue < converter.\mbox{\hyperlink{a00105_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce_a160d6366514b7fe5ec086f528835c5ce}{decimal}}) \{    \textcolor{comment}{// correct for rounding errors}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01097}01097     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_a3cdcf6a32941852a0f72b81e84d97928_a3cdcf6a32941852a0f72b81e84d97928}{IS\_FLAG\_SET}}(flags, \mbox{\hyperlink{a00008_ac9e43acba426d73c5f42d4a50826b023_ac9e43acba426d73c5f42d4a50826b023ab22da515aa39ad217723d1a95c2fa124}{ADAPTIVE\_EXPONENT\_FLAG}})) \{   \textcolor{comment}{// in "{}\%g"{} mode, "{}precision"{} is the number of "{}significant figures"{} not decimals}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01108}01108     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01109}01109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{a00008_source_l01110}01110     \textcolor{comment}{// check that everything fits}}
